```

Wait, let me double-check the relationship format. According to the instructions, I need to use the format "[Character Name] is to [Character Name]: [relationship]" and specifically, the relationship should be directed FROM the current character TO the other character.

So for Jasmine to John, it would be "Jasmine is to John: confidant" or "Jasmine is to John: someone she confides in".

Actually, looking at the messages, it seems like Jasmine is coming to John for help, so John might be more like a confidant or support person. "Jasmine is to John: confidant" or "Jasmine is to John: person she seeks help from" would work.

But I should also consider that John appears to know Jasmine well enough that she feels comfortable coming to him with this embarrassing issue, so the relationship might be a friend.

For now, I'll use "Jasmine is to John: confidant" as a safe option.
